<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:март.html>март</a> (2360)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мартъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">martŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Old Church Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">мартъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">martŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Μάρτιος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Mártios</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mārtius</i>, from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Mavors</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:март.html>март</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mart</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:март.html>ма́рта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:март.html>ма́рты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:март.html>ма́ртов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>March

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мартышка.html>марты́шка</a> (9329)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мартышка.html>марты́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">martýška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мартышка.html>марты́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мартышка.html>марты́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мартышка.html>марты́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>marmoset, monkey</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:марш.html>марш</a> (3688)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">marche</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">march</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">marsz</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Marsch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:марш.html>марш</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">marš</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:марш.html>ма́рша</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:марш.html>ма́рши</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:марш.html>ма́ршей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>march
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похоронный.html>похоро́нный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:марш.html>марш</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">poxorónnyj <b>marš</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">funeral march</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> march</li>
<li>flight of stairs</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>forward! (command)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:старт.html>старт</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:внимание.html>внима́ние</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:марш.html>марш</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na start, vnimánije, <b>marš</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ready, set, go!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>ша́гом</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:марш.html>марш</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">šágom <b>marš</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">quick march!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:марш.html>марш</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отсюда.html>отсю́да</a>!</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>marš</b> otsjúda!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">off you go!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>кругом</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:марш.html>марш</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krugom <b>marš</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">backward march!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***маршировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:маршировать.html>марширова́ть</a> (14257)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">marcher</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">marschieren</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маршировать.html>марширова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">marširovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to march</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маскарад.html>маскара́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">maskarád</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маскарад.html>маскара́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маскарад.html>маскара́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маскарад.html>маскара́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>masquerade, masked ball</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:масленица.html>ма́сленица</a> (31012)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*maslěnica</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*maslěnъjь</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ica</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*maslo</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масленица.html>ма́сленица</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">máslenica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масленица.html>ма́сленицы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масленица.html>ма́сленицы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масленица.html>ма́слениц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative letter-case form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масленица.html>ма́сленица</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Máslenica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>; Maslenitsa, Shrovetide, Butter Week, Crepe Week <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">the week before Lent, seven weeks before Easter</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> feast, high life
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:житье.html>житьё</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:масленица.html>ма́сленица</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne žitʹjó, a <b>máslenica</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">a bed of roses; living high on the hog</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кот.html>коту́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:масленица.html>ма́сленица</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>придёт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:великий.html>вели́кий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пост.html>пост</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne vsjó kotú <b>máslenica</b>, pridjót i velíkij post</i> ― <span class="e-translation">good things don’t last forever (after dinner comes the reckoning)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">regional<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> butter churn</li></ol>

***масло.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:масло.html>ма́сло</a> (1393)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:масло.html>ма́сло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">maslo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*maslo</i>. Related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мазать.html>ма́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mázatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to smear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масло.html>ма́сло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">máslo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масло.html>ма́сла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масло.html>масла́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масло.html>ма́сел</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>butter</li>
<li>oil <i>(vegetable or mineral)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растительный.html>расти́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:масло.html>ма́сло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rastítelʹnoje máslo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">vegetable oil</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маслянистый.html>масляни́стый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">masljanístyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)масляни́стее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)масляни́стей</b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масса.html>ма́сса</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mássa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масса.html>ма́ссы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масса.html>ма́ссы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масса.html>ма́сс</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mass</li>
<li>mass, paste</li>
<li>mass, bulk</li>
<li>ground (electrical)</li></ol>

***массировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:массировать.html>масси́ровать</a> (20698)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">massieren</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:массировать.html>масси́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">massírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to massage</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Can also be used with perfective meaning in the past tense.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масса.html>ма́сса</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mássa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:массовый.html>ма́ссовый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mássovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mass, bulk
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:массовый.html>ма́ссовое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:убийство.html>уби́йство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mássovoje</b> ubíjstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>mass</b> murder</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mass; <a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:массовый.html>ма́ссовая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:культура.html>культу́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mássovaja</b> kulʹtúra</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>mass</b> culture, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a></b> culture</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
